int sensorvalue2=0;

void setup()
{
  Serial.begin(9600);
  pinMode(A0,INPUT);
  pinMode(A1,INPUT);
  pinMode(13,INPUT);
}
void loop()
{
  //for sensor one
  sensorvalue1=analogRead(A0);
  int voltage1=sensorvalue1*(5000/1024.0);
  int temp1=(voltage1-500)/10;
  Serial.print("Temperature:");
  Serial.println(temp1);
  //for sensor two
  sensorvalue2=analogRead(A0);
  int voltage2=sensorvalue2*(5000/1024.0);
  int temp2=(voltage2-500)/10;
  Serial.print("Temperature:");
  Serial.println(temp2);
  if(temp1>=60 && temp2>=80)
  {
    digitalWrite(led,HIGH);
  }
  else
    digitalWrite(led,LOW);
}

}

27/03/23, 9:41 am - +91 96539 41757: #include <Adafruit_MPU6050.h>
#include <Adafruit_Sensor.h>
#include <Wire.h>
Adafruit_MPU6050 mpu;
void setup() {
  Serial.begin(115200);
  if (!mpu.begin()) {
    Serial.println("Failed to find MPU6050 chip");
    while (1) {
      delay(10);
    }
  }
  Serial.println("MPU6050 Found!");
   
  mpu.setAccelerometerRange(MPU6050_RANGE_8_G);  
  mpu.setGyroRange(MPU6050_RANGE_500_DEG);
  mpu.setFilterBandwidth(MPU6050_BAND_21_HZ);
  delay(100);
}
void loop() {
  sensors_event_t a, g, temp;
  mpu.getEvent(&a, &g, &temp);
  Serial.print("Rotation X: ");
  Serial.print(g.gyro.x);
  Serial.print(", Y: ");
  Serial.print(g.gyro.y);
  Serial.print(", Z: ");
  Serial.print(g.gyro.z);
  Serial.println(" rad/s");
  Serial.print("Temperature: ");
  Serial.print(temp.temperature);
  Serial.println(" degC");
  delay(500);
  
}

06/11/23, 9:10 am - Amit Pal: 3. The correct way to create a function in Python is:
```python
def myFunction():
```

4. The correct NumPy function to calculate the mean of an array is `average`.

5. The character used to give single-line comments in Python is `#`.

6. The correct syntax for creating a pandas DataFrame is:
```python
pd.DataFrame(dict)
```

7. To count the total number of values in a list, you can use the `len()` function.

8. A DataFrame object can be created using a Python Dictionary.

9. The result of `np.array([1, 2, 3]) * 32` is `[32, 64, 96]`.

10. A DataFrame is a two-dimensional tabular data structure with labeled axes.

11. The correct syntax to check the number of dimensions in an array is `arr.ndim`.

12. `print` is a built-in function in Python.

13. The function used to load data from a CSV file into a DataFrame in Pandas is `read_csv`.

14. A two-dimensional array is represented as:
```python
[[1, 2, 3],
 [4, 5, 6]]
```

18/05/24, 9:22 am - Harshita Invertis: #include <stdio.h>
#include <ctype.h>

int main() {
    char str[100];
    int i, vowels = 0, consonants = 0, digits = 0, spaces = 0, others = 0;

    printf("Enter a string: ");
    fgets(str, sizeof str, stdin);

    for(i = 0; str[i] != '\0'; ++i) {
        if(isalpha(str[i])) {
            if(str[i] == 'a' || str[i] == 'e' || str[i] == 'i' || str[i] == 'o' || str[i] == 'u' ||
               str[i] == 'A' || str[i] == 'E' || str[i] == 'I' || str[i] == 'O' || str[i] == 'U') {
                ++vowels;
            } else {
                ++consonants;
            }
        } else if(isdigit(str[i])) {
            ++digits;
        } else if(isspace(str[i])) {
            ++spaces;
        } else {
            ++others;
        }
    }

    printf("Number of vowels: %d\n", vowels);
    printf("Number of consonants: %d\n", consonants);
    printf("Number of digits: %d\n", digits);
    printf("Number of spaces: %d\n", spaces);
    printf("Number of other characters: %d\n", others);

    return 0;
}

18/05/24, 9:42 am - +91 87368 71556: Distributed bootstrapping leverages multiple machines to accelerate the process by splitting the workload. Here's a common scenario using MPI (Message Passing Interface) for parallel computing:
 * Initial Setup: Each machine loads a portion of the data to be resampled.
 * Resampling: Machines independently perform bootstrap resamples on their assigned data subsets.
 * Data Exchange: Machines exchange resampled datasets efficiently using MPI communication primitives.
 * Local Analysis: Each machine analyzes the received resampled datasets to compute statistics or build models.
 * Global Aggregation: Results from all machines are aggregated using MPI collective operations to obtain final statistics or a combined model.
This approach significantly reduces bootstrapping time by utilizing the combined processing power of multiple machines.

29/06/24, 12:56 pm - +91 77590 39741: Selling a paid course involves several strategies to showcase its value and reach potential customers. Here's a step-by-step guide to help you get started:

1. *Define your target audience*: Identify who would benefit from your course and create buyer personas.
2. *Highlight the benefits*: Emphasize the skills or knowledge students will gain and how it will improve their lives or careers.
3. *Create a compelling sales page*: Showcase the course content, format, and testimonials. Use persuasive copywriting and eye-catching visuals.
4. *Set a competitive price*: Research similar courses and price yours appropriately.
5. *Choose a sales platform*: Utilize platforms like Udemy, Teachable, or Kajabi to host and sell your course.
6. *Develop a marketing strategy*:
    - Utilize social media and email marketing.
    - Collaborate with influencers or affiliates.
    - Run paid advertisements (Google Ads, Facebook Ads).
    - Offer free previews or trials.
7. *Provide excellent customer support*: Ensure a smooth learning experience and address any customer inquiries.
8. *Collect and showcase testimonials*: Share feedback and success stories from satisfied students.
9. *Continuously improve and update*: Refine your course content and marketing strategy based on feedback and market trends.

Remember, selling a paid course requires ongoing effort and optimization. Focus on providing value to your students, and with the right strategies, you'll increase your chances of success!
